<CodeSampleTabbedSection>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-get_workflows_v1_workflows_get_code-samples_typescript"
  tags={{"codeSample":"typescript"}}
>

TypeScript

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-get_workflows_v1_workflows_get_code-samples_typescript"
>

<CodeSample>

```typescript
import { Mistral } from "@mistralai/mistralai";

const mistral = new Mistral({
  apiKey: "MISTRAL_API_KEY",
});

async function run() {
  const result = await mistral.workflows.getWorkflows({});

  for await (const page of result) {
    console.log(page);
  }
}

run();

```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-get_workflows_v1_workflows_get_code-samples_python"
  tags={{"codeSample":"python"}}
>

Python

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-get_workflows_v1_workflows_get_code-samples_python"
>

<CodeSample>

```python
from mistralai.client import Mistral
import os


with Mistral(
    api_key=os.getenv("MISTRAL_API_KEY", ""),
) as mistral:

    res = mistral.workflows.get_workflows(include_shared=True, order="asc", limit=50, active_only=False)

    while res is not None:
        # Handle items

        res = res.next()


```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"

TypeScript

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-get_workflow_registrations_v1_workflows_registrations_get_code-samples_typescript"
>

<CodeSample>

```typescript
import { Mistral } from "@mistralai/mistralai";

const mistral = new Mistral({
  apiKey: "MISTRAL_API_KEY",
});

async function run() {
  const result = await mistral.workflows.getWorkflowRegistrations({});

  console.log(result);
}

run();

```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-get_workflow_registrations_v1_workflows_registrations_get_code-samples_python"
  tags={{"codeSample":"python"}}
>

Python

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-get_workflow_registrations_v1_workflows_registrations_get_code-samples_python"
>

<CodeSample>

```python
from mistralai.client import Mistral
import os


with Mistral(
    api_key=os.getenv("MISTRAL_API_KEY", ""),
) as mistral:

    res = mistral.workflows.get_workflow_registrations(active_only=False, include_shared=True, with_workflow=False, limit=50)

    # Handle response
    print(res)


```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

  slot="tab"
  id="operation-get_workflow_registrations_v1_workflows_registrations_get_code-samples_curl"

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /v1/workflows/\{workflow\_identifier\}/execute \{#operation-execute_workflow_v1_workflows_workflow_identifier_execute_post\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Execute Workflow_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Execute Workflow

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

<CodeSampleTabbedSection>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-execute_workflow_v1_workflows_workflow_identifier_execute_post_code-samples_typescript"
  tags={{"codeSample":"typescript"}}
>

TypeScript

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-execute_workflow_v1_workflows_workflow_identifier_execute_post_code-samples_typescript"
>

<CodeSample>

```typescript
import { Mistral } from "@mistralai/mistralai";

const mistral = new Mistral({
  apiKey: "MISTRAL_API_KEY",
});

async function run() {
  const result = await mistral.workflows.executeWorkflow({
    workflowIdentifier: "<value>",
    workflowExecutionRequest: {},
  });

  console.log(result);
}

run();

```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-execute_workflow_v1_workflows_workflow_identifier_execute_post_code-samples_python"
  tags={{"codeSample":"python"}}
>

Python

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-execute_workflow_v1_workflows_workflow_identifier_execute_post_code-samples_python"
>

<CodeSample>

```python
from mistralai.client import Mistral
import os


with Mistral(
    api_key=os.getenv("MISTRAL_API_KEY", ""),
) as mistral:

    res = mistral.workflows.execute_workflow(workflow_identifier="<value>", wait_for_result=False)

    # Handle response
    print(res)


```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-execute_workflow_v1_workflows_workflow_identifier_execute_post_code-samples_curl"
  tags={{"codeSample":"curl"}}

```curl
curl https://api.mistral.ai/v1/workflows/{workflow_identifier}/execute \
 -X POST \
 -H 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_APIKEY_HERE' \
 -H 'Content-Type: application/json' \
 -d '{}'
```

```json
}
```

```python
from mistralai.client import Mistral
import os


with Mistral(
```

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-get_workflow_v1_workflows_workflow_identifier_get_code-samples_typescript"
>

<CodeSample>

```typescript
import { Mistral } from "@mistralai/mistralai";

const mistral = new Mistral({
  apiKey: "MISTRAL_API_KEY",
});

async function run() {
  const result = await mistral.workflows.getWorkflow({
    workflowIdentifier: "<value>",
  });

  console.log(result);
}

run();

```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-get_workflow_v1_workflows_workflow_identifier_get_code-samples_python"

Python

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-get_workflow_v1_workflows_workflow_identifier_get_code-samples_python"
>

<CodeSample>

```python
from mistralai.client import Mistral
import os


with Mistral(
    api_key=os.getenv("MISTRAL_API_KEY", ""),
) as mistral:

    res = mistral.workflows.get_workflow(workflow_identifier="<value>")

    # Handle response
    print(res)


```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>GET</b></Pill> /v1/workflows/registrations/\{workflow\_registration\_id\} \{#operation-get_workflow_registration_v1_workflows_registrations_workflow_registration_id_get\}

  tags={{"codeSample":"typescript"}}
>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-get_workflow_registration_v1_workflows_registrations_workflow_registration_id_get_code-samples_typescript"

<CodeSample>

```typescript
import { Mistral } from "@mistralai/mistralai";

const mistral = new Mistral({
  apiKey: "MISTRAL_API_KEY",
});

async function run() {
  const result = await mistral.workflows.getWorkflowRegistration({
    workflowRegistrationId: "c4d86c40-960f-4e9a-9d6f-ad8342d7aa83",
  });

  console.log(result);
}

run();

```

```python
from mistralai.client import Mistral
import os


with Mistral(
    api_key=os.getenv("MISTRAL_API_KEY", ""),
) as mistral:

    res = mistral.workflows.get_workflow_registration(workflow_registration_id="c4d86c40-960f-4e9a-9d6f-ad8342d7aa83", with_workflow=False, include_shared=True)

    # Handle response
    print(res)


```

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>PUT</b></Pill> /v1/workflows/archive \{#operation-bulk_archive_workflows_v1_workflows_archive_put\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Bulk Archive Workflows_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Bulk Archive Workflows

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

<CodeSampleTabbedSection>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-bulk_archive_workflows_v1_workflows_archive_put_code-samples_typescript"
  tags={{"codeSample":"typescript"}}
>

TypeScript

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-bulk_archive_workflows_v1_workflows_archive_put_code-samples_typescript"
>

<CodeSample>

```typescript
import { Mistral } from "@mistralai/mistralai";

const mistral = new Mistral({
  apiKey: "MISTRAL_API_KEY",
});

async function run() {
  const result = await mistral.workflows.bulkArchiveWorkflows({
    workflowIds: [],
  });

  console.log(result);
}

run();

```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-bulk_archive_workflows_v1_workflows_archive_put_code-samples_python"
  tags={{"codeSample":"python"}}
>

Python

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-bulk_archive_workflows_v1_workflows_archive_put_code-samples_python"
>

<CodeSample>

```python
from mistralai.client import Mistral
import os


with Mistral(
    api_key=os.getenv("MISTRAL_API_KEY", ""),
) as mistral:

    res = mistral.workflows.bulk_archive_workflows(workflow_ids=[])

    # Handle response
    print(res)


```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-bulk_archive_workflows_v1_workflows_archive_put_code-samples_curl"
  tags={{"codeSample":"curl"}}
>

cURL

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-bulk_archive_workflows_v1_workflows_archive_put_code-samples_curl"
>

<CodeSample>

```curl
curl https://api.mistral.ai/v1/workflows/archive \
 -X PUT \
 -H 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_APIKEY_HERE' \
 -H 'Content-Type: application/json' \
 -d '{
  "workflow_ids": [
    "019b2bd7-96e7-7219-8c0b-45a73da50088"
  ]
}'
```

</CodeSample>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>PUT</b></Pill> /v1/workflows/unarchive \{#operation-bulk_unarchive_workflows_v1_workflows_unarchive_put\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Bulk Unarchive Workflows_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Bulk Unarchive Workflows

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

<CodeSampleTabbedSection>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-bulk_unarchive_workflows_v1_workflows_unarchive_put_code-samples_typescript"
  tags={{"codeSample":"typescript"}}
>

TypeScript

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-bulk_unarchive_workflows_v1_workflows_unarchive_put_code-samples_typescript"
>

<CodeSample>

```typescript
import { Mistral } from "@mistralai/mistralai";

const mistral = new Mistral({
  apiKey: "MISTRAL_API_KEY",
});

async function run() {
  const result = await mistral.workflows.bulkUnarchiveWorkflows({
    workflowIds: [],
  });

  console.log(result);
}

run();

```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-bulk_unarchive_workflows_v1_workflows_unarchive_put_code-samples_python"
  tags={{"codeSample":"python"}}
>

Python

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-bulk_unarchive_workflows_v1_workflows_unarchive_put_code-samples_python"
>

<CodeSample>

```python
from mistralai.client import Mistral
import os


with Mistral(
    api_key=os.getenv("MISTRAL_API_KEY", ""),
) as mistral:

    res = mistral.workflows.bulk_unarchive_workflows(workflow_ids=[])

    # Handle response
    print(res)


```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-bulk_unarchive_workflows_v1_workflows_unarchive_put_code-samples_curl"
  tags={{"codeSample":"curl"}}
>

cURL

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-bulk_unarchive_workflows_v1_workflows_unarchive_put_code-samples_curl"
>

<CodeSample>

```curl
curl https://api.mistral.ai/v1/workflows/unarchive \
 -X PUT \
 -H 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_APIKEY_HERE' \
 -H 'Content-Type: application/json' \
 -d '{
  "workflow_ids": [
    "019b2bd7-96e7-7219-8c0b-45a73da50088"
  ]
}'
```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

</CodeSampleTabbedSection>

</OperationCodeSamplesSection>

<OperationRequestBodyExamplesSection slot="request-body-examples">

<Section>

<SectionTitle slot="title">

### Request Example \{#operation-bulk_unarchive_workflows_v1_workflows_unarchive_put_request-examples\}

</SectionTitle>

<SectionContent slot="content">

```json
{
  "workflow_ids": [
    "019b2bd7-96e7-7219-8c0b-45a73da50088"
  ]
```

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>PUT</b></Pill> /v1/workflows/\{workflow\_identifier\}/archive \{#operation-archive_workflow_v1_workflows_workflow_identifier_archive_put\}

</OperationTitleSection>

_Archive Workflow_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Archive Workflow

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

<CodeSampleTabbedSection>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-archive_workflow_v1_workflows_workflow_identifier_archive_put_code-samples_typescript"
  tags={{"codeSample":"typescript"}}
>

TypeScript

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-archive_workflow_v1_workflows_workflow_identifier_archive_put_code-samples_typescript"
>

<CodeSample>

```typescript
import { Mistral } from "@mistralai/mistralai";

const mistral = new Mistral({
  apiKey: "MISTRAL_API_KEY",
});

async function run() {
  const result = await mistral.workflows.archiveWorkflow({
    workflowIdentifier: "<value>",
  });

  console.log(result);
}

run();

```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-archive_workflow_v1_workflows_workflow_identifier_archive_put_code-samples_python"
  tags={{"codeSample":"python"}}
>

Python

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-archive_workflow_v1_workflows_workflow_identifier_archive_put_code-samples_python"
>

<CodeSample>

```python
from mistralai.client import Mistral
import os


with Mistral(
    api_key=os.getenv("MISTRAL_API_KEY", ""),
) as mistral:

    res = mistral.workflows.archive_workflow(workflow_identifier="<value>")

    # Handle response
    print(res)


```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

  slot="tab"

```curl
curl https://api.mistral.ai/v1/workflows/{workflow_identifier}/archive \

 -H 'Content-Type: application/json'
```

```typescript
import { Mistral } from "@mistralai/mistralai";

const mistral = new Mistral({
  apiKey: "MISTRAL_API_KEY",
});

async function run() {
  const result = await mistral.workflows.unarchiveWorkflow({
    workflowIdentifier: "<value>",
  });

  console.log(result);
}

run();

```

```python
from mistralai.client import Mistral
import os


with Mistral(
    api_key=os.getenv("MISTRAL_API_KEY", ""),
) as mistral:

    res = mistral.workflows.unarchive_workflow(workflow_identifier="<value>")

    # Handle response
    print(res)


```
